-- Add double quotes to protect funky column names
-- Add a further UNPIVOT to create an ExampleData column

USE DATABASE SHARED_SANDBOX
;

USE SCHEMA OSC_DATA_EXTRACTS
;

SELECT query_to_run || ' ORDER BY TableName, ColPos;'
FROM (
    SELECT LISTAGG(TableQuery, ' UNION ALL ') AS query_to_run
    FROM (
        SELECT '
    SELECT
      TableName
      ,TotalRows
      ,SUBSTRING(pCol, 2, CHARINDEX(''__'', pCol) - 1) AS ColName
      ,CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX(''__'', pCol) + 2) as INTEGER) AS ColPos
      ,NullCount
      ,CAST(CAST(NullCount AS DECIMAL(12,2)) / NULLIF(CAST(TotalRows AS DECIMAL(12,2)),0) * 100.00 AS DECIMAL(12,2)) AS NullPct
      ,ExampleData
    FROM (
        SELECT
          ''' || t.TABLE_NAME || ''' AS TableName,
          COUNT(*) AS TotalRows,
          ' || LISTAGG('COUNT(*) - COUNT("' || c.COLUMN_NAME || '") AS "p' || c.COLUMN_NAME || '__' || c.ORDINAL_POSITION, '",') || '",

          ' || LISTAGG('IFNULL((SELECT TOP 1 "' || c.COLUMN_NAME || '" FROM ' || t.TABLE_NAME || ' WHERE "' || c.COLUMN_NAME || '" IS NOT NULL), '''') AS "q' || c.COLUMN_NAME || '__' || c.ORDINAL_POSITION, '",') || '"
          
        FROM ' || t.TABLE_SCHEMA || '.' || t.TABLE_NAME || '
        ) AS t
    UNPIVOT (NullCount FOR pCol IN 
        (' || LISTAGG('"p' || CAST(c.COLUMN_NAME AS varchar()) || '__' || CAST(c.ORDINAL_POSITION AS varchar()), '",') || '")
    ) AS p

    UNPIVOT(ExampleData FOR qCol IN
        (' || LISTAGG('"q' || CAST(c.COLUMN_NAME AS varchar()) || '__' || CAST(c.ORDINAL_POSITION AS varchar()), '",') || '")
    ) AS q
    WHERE CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX(''__'', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) = CAST(SUBSTRING(qCol, CHARINDEX(''__'', qCol) + 2) AS INTEGER)'
    
            FROM SHARED_SANDBOX.INFORMATION_SCHEMA.TABLES t
            INNER JOIN INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS c ON c.TABLE_NAME = t.TABLE_NAME AND c.TABLE_SCHEMA = t.TABLE_SCHEMA
            WHERE t.TABLE_SCHEMA = 'OSC_DATA_EXTRACTS'
                --AND t.TABLE_NAME = 'SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_OBJ' OR t.TABLE_NAME = 'SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS'
                --AND t.TABLE_NAME = 'SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_ORG_PROF'
            GROUP BY t.TABLE_NAME, t.TABLE_SCHEMA
    
        ) AS t(TableQuery)
) AS generate
;


-- Format the output with Poor SQL


SELECT TableName
	,TotalRows
	,SUBSTRING(pCol, 2, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) - 1) AS ColName
	,CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) AS ColPos
	,NullCount
	,CAST(CAST(NullCount AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) / NULLIF(CAST(TotalRows AS DECIMAL(12, 2)), 0) * 100.00 AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) AS NullPct
	,ExampleData
FROM (
	SELECT 'SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS' AS TableName
		,COUNT(*) AS TotalRows
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Show Time As") AS "pShow Time As__1"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("ACTIVITY_ID") AS "pACTIVITY_ID__3"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Activity.Assignee Attendee (Flag)") AS "pActivity.Assignee Attendee (Flag)__10"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Activity.Assignee Last Updated By (GID) (PII)") AS "pActivity.Assignee Last Updated By (GID) (PII)__7"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Activity.Assignee Created Timestamp") AS "pActivity.Assignee Created Timestamp__8"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("EMPLOYEE_ID") AS "pEMPLOYEE_ID__2"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Activity.Assignee Created By (GID) (PII)") AS "pActivity.Assignee Created By (GID) (PII)__9"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Activity.Assignee Last Updated Timestamp") AS "pActivity.Assignee Last Updated Timestamp__6"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Activity.Assignee User Last Updated Timestamp") AS "pActivity.Assignee User Last Updated Timestamp__5"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Activity.Assignee.Response") AS "pActivity.Assignee.Response__4"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Show Time As"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
				WHERE "Show Time As" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qShow Time As__1"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "ACTIVITY_ID"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
				WHERE "ACTIVITY_ID" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qACTIVITY_ID__3"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Activity.Assignee Attendee (Flag)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
				WHERE "Activity.Assignee Attendee (Flag)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qActivity.Assignee Attendee (Flag)__10"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Activity.Assignee Last Updated By (GID) (PII)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
				WHERE "Activity.Assignee Last Updated By (GID) (PII)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qActivity.Assignee Last Updated By (GID) (PII)__7"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Activity.Assignee Created Timestamp"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
				WHERE "Activity.Assignee Created Timestamp" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qActivity.Assignee Created Timestamp__8"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "EMPLOYEE_ID"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
				WHERE "EMPLOYEE_ID" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qEMPLOYEE_ID__2"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Activity.Assignee Created By (GID) (PII)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
				WHERE "Activity.Assignee Created By (GID) (PII)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qActivity.Assignee Created By (GID) (PII)__9"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Activity.Assignee Last Updated Timestamp"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
				WHERE "Activity.Assignee Last Updated Timestamp" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qActivity.Assignee Last Updated Timestamp__6"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Activity.Assignee User Last Updated Timestamp"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
				WHERE "Activity.Assignee User Last Updated Timestamp" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qActivity.Assignee User Last Updated Timestamp__5"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Activity.Assignee.Response"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
				WHERE "Activity.Assignee.Response" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qActivity.Assignee.Response__4"
	FROM OSC_DATA_EXTRACTS.SV_OSC_P_T_ACT_ASS
	) AS t
UNPIVOT(NullCount FOR pCol IN (
			"pShow Time As__1"
			,"pACTIVITY_ID__3"
			,"pActivity.Assignee Attendee (Flag)__10"
			,"pActivity.Assignee Last Updated By (GID) (PII)__7"
			,"pActivity.Assignee Created Timestamp__8"
			,"pEMPLOYEE_ID__2"
			,"pActivity.Assignee Created By (GID) (PII)__9"
			,"pActivity.Assignee Last Updated Timestamp__6"
			,"pActivity.Assignee User Last Updated Timestamp__5"
			,"pActivity.Assignee.Response__4"
			)) AS p
UNPIVOT(ExampleData FOR qCol IN (
			"qShow Time As__1"
			,"qACTIVITY_ID__3"
			,"qActivity.Assignee Attendee (Flag)__10"
			,"qActivity.Assignee Last Updated By (GID) (PII)__7"
			,"qActivity.Assignee Created Timestamp__8"
			,"qEMPLOYEE_ID__2"
			,"qActivity.Assignee Created By (GID) (PII)__9"
			,"qActivity.Assignee Last Updated Timestamp__6"
			,"qActivity.Assignee User Last Updated Timestamp__5"
			,"qActivity.Assignee.Response__4"
			)) AS q
WHERE CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) = CAST(SUBSTRING(qCol, CHARINDEX('__', qCol) + 2) AS INTEGER)

UNION ALL

SELECT TableName
	,TotalRows
	,SUBSTRING(pCol, 2, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) - 1) AS ColName
	,CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) AS ColPos
	,NullCount
	,CAST(CAST(NullCount AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) / NULLIF(CAST(TotalRows AS DECIMAL(12, 2)), 0) * 100.00 AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) AS NullPct
	,ExampleData
FROM (
	SELECT 'SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_RESOURCE' AS TableName
		,COUNT(*) AS TotalRows
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Access") AS "pAccess__1"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("SALESACCOUNT_ID") AS "pSALESACCOUNT_ID__2"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Function (Position Type)") AS "pFunction (Position Type)__3"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("EMPLOYEE_ID") AS "pEMPLOYEE_ID__4"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Access"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_RESOURCE
				WHERE "Access" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qAccess__1"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "SALESACCOUNT_ID"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_RESOURCE
				WHERE "SALESACCOUNT_ID" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qSALESACCOUNT_ID__2"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Function (Position Type)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_RESOURCE
				WHERE "Function (Position Type)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qFunction (Position Type)__3"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "EMPLOYEE_ID"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_RESOURCE
				WHERE "EMPLOYEE_ID" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qEMPLOYEE_ID__4"
	FROM OSC_DATA_EXTRACTS.SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_RESOURCE
	) AS t
UNPIVOT(NullCount FOR pCol IN (
			"pAccess__1"
			,"pSALESACCOUNT_ID__2"
			,"pFunction (Position Type)__3"
			,"pEMPLOYEE_ID__4"
			)) AS p
UNPIVOT(ExampleData FOR qCol IN (
			"qAccess__1"
			,"qSALESACCOUNT_ID__2"
			,"qFunction (Position Type)__3"
			,"qEMPLOYEE_ID__4"
			)) AS q
WHERE CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) = CAST(SUBSTRING(qCol, CHARINDEX('__', qCol) + 2) AS INTEGER)

UNION ALL

SELECT TableName
	,TotalRows
	,SUBSTRING(pCol, 2, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) - 1) AS ColName
	,CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) AS ColPos
	,NullCount
	,CAST(CAST(NullCount AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) / NULLIF(CAST(TotalRows AS DECIMAL(12, 2)), 0) * 100.00 AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) AS NullPct
	,ExampleData
FROM (
	SELECT 'SV_OSC_P_T_TERR_ACCOUNT' AS TableName
		,COUNT(*) AS TotalRows
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("SALESACCOUNT_ID") AS "pSALESACCOUNT_ID__2"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("TERRITORYVERSION_ID") AS "pTERRITORYVERSION_ID__1"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "SALESACCOUNT_ID"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_TERR_ACCOUNT
				WHERE "SALESACCOUNT_ID" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qSALESACCOUNT_ID__2"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "TERRITORYVERSION_ID"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_TERR_ACCOUNT
				WHERE "TERRITORYVERSION_ID" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qTERRITORYVERSION_ID__1"
	FROM OSC_DATA_EXTRACTS.SV_OSC_P_T_TERR_ACCOUNT
	) AS t
UNPIVOT(NullCount FOR pCol IN (
			"pSALESACCOUNT_ID__2"
			,"pTERRITORYVERSION_ID__1"
			)) AS p
UNPIVOT(ExampleData FOR qCol IN (
			"qSALESACCOUNT_ID__2"
			,"qTERRITORYVERSION_ID__1"
			)) AS q
WHERE CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) = CAST(SUBSTRING(qCol, CHARINDEX('__', qCol) + 2) AS INTEGER)

UNION ALL

SELECT TableName
	,TotalRows
	,SUBSTRING(pCol, 2, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) - 1) AS ColName
	,CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) AS ColPos
	,NullCount
	,CAST(CAST(NullCount AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) / NULLIF(CAST(TotalRows AS DECIMAL(12, 2)), 0) * 100.00 AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) AS NullPct
	,ExampleData
FROM (
	SELECT 'SV_OSC_P_T_EMP_RESOURCE' AS TableName

		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("EMPLOYEE_ID (Manager)") AS "pEMPLOYEE_ID (Manager)__3"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Employee.Geography") AS "pEmployee.Geography__11"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Employee.User_Name (PII)") AS "pEmployee.User_Name (PII)__5"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Employee.Job Title (PII)") AS "pEmployee.Job Title (PII)__10"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Employee.Last Updated Timestamp") AS "pEmployee.Last Updated Timestamp__8"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Employee (GID) (PII)") AS "pEmployee (GID) (PII)__15"

				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_EMP_RESOURCE

				), '') AS "qEmployee.Last Name (PII)__9"

				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_EMP_RESOURCE

				), '') AS "qEMPLOYEE_ID (Manager)__3"

			,"qEMPLOYEE_ID__4"
			)) AS q
WHERE CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) = CAST(SUBSTRING(qCol, CHARINDEX('__', qCol) + 2) AS INTEGER)

UNION ALL

SELECT TableName
	,TotalRows
	,SUBSTRING(pCol, 2, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) - 1) AS ColName
	,CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) AS ColPos
	,NullCount
	,CAST(CAST(NullCount AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) / NULLIF(CAST(TotalRows AS DECIMAL(12, 2)), 0) * 100.00 AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) AS NullPct
	,ExampleData
FROM (
	SELECT 'SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE' AS TableName
		,COUNT(*) AS TotalRows
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone Created Timestamp") AS "pContact.Phone Created Timestamp__9"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone Type") AS "pContact.Phone Type__3"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone Primary (Flag)") AS "pContact.Phone Primary (Flag)__5"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("CONTACT_ID") AS "pCONTACT_ID__2"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("CONTACT_PHONE_ID") AS "pCONTACT_PHONE_ID__1"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone Status") AS "pContact.Phone Status__4"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone Last Updated By (GID) (PII)") AS "pContact.Phone Last Updated By (GID) (PII)__7"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone Area Code") AS "pContact.Phone Area Code__12"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone Last Updated Timestamp") AS "pContact.Phone Last Updated Timestamp__6"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone Extension") AS "pContact.Phone Extension__8"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone (PII)") AS "pContact.Phone (PII)__13"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone Created By (GID) (PII)") AS "pContact.Phone Created By (GID) (PII)__10"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Contact.Phone Country Code") AS "pContact.Phone Country Code__11"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone Created Timestamp"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone Created Timestamp" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone Created Timestamp__9"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone Type"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone Type" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone Type__3"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone Primary (Flag)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone Primary (Flag)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone Primary (Flag)__5"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "CONTACT_ID"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "CONTACT_ID" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qCONTACT_ID__2"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "CONTACT_PHONE_ID"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "CONTACT_PHONE_ID" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qCONTACT_PHONE_ID__1"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone Status"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone Status" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone Status__4"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone Last Updated By (GID) (PII)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone Last Updated By (GID) (PII)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone Last Updated By (GID) (PII)__7"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone Area Code"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone Area Code" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone Area Code__12"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone Last Updated Timestamp"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone Last Updated Timestamp" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone Last Updated Timestamp__6"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone Extension"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone Extension" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone Extension__8"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone (PII)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone (PII)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone (PII)__13"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone Created By (GID) (PII)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone Created By (GID) (PII)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone Created By (GID) (PII)__10"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Contact.Phone Country Code"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
				WHERE "Contact.Phone Country Code" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qContact.Phone Country Code__11"
	FROM OSC_DATA_EXTRACTS.SV_OSC_P_T_CON_PHONE
	) AS t
UNPIVOT(NullCount FOR pCol IN (
			"pContact.Phone Created Timestamp__9"
			,"pContact.Phone Type__3"
			,"pContact.Phone Primary (Flag)__5"
			,"pCONTACT_ID__2"
			,"pCONTACT_PHONE_ID__1"
			,"pContact.Phone Status__4"
			,"pContact.Phone Last Updated By (GID) (PII)__7"

	,TotalRows

SELECT TableName
	,TotalRows
	,SUBSTRING(pCol, 2, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) - 1) AS ColName
	,CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) AS ColPos
	,NullCount
	,CAST(CAST(NullCount AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) / NULLIF(CAST(TotalRows AS DECIMAL(12, 2)), 0) * 100.00 AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) AS NullPct
	,ExampleData
FROM (
	SELECT 'SV_OSC_P_T_ASS_OPTY_REL' AS TableName
		,COUNT(*) AS TotalRows
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Relationship Type") AS "pRelationship Type__2"

SELECT TableName
	,TotalRows
	,SUBSTRING(pCol, 2, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) - 1) AS ColName
	,CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) AS ColPos
	,NullCount
	,CAST(CAST(NullCount AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) / NULLIF(CAST(TotalRows AS DECIMAL(12, 2)), 0) * 100.00 AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) AS NullPct
	,ExampleData
FROM (
	SELECT 'SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_CLASS' AS TableName
		,COUNT(*) AS TotalRows
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("ACCOUNT_ID") AS "pACCOUNT_ID__1"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Account Classification.Primary (Flag)") AS "pAccount Classification.Primary (Flag)__3"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Account Classification.Classification Category") AS "pAccount Classification.Classification Category__4"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Account Classification.Assignment Criteria") AS "pAccount Classification.Assignment Criteria__5"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("Account Classification.Status") AS "pAccount Classification.Status__2"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "ACCOUNT_ID"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_CLASS
				WHERE "ACCOUNT_ID" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qACCOUNT_ID__1"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Account Classification.Primary (Flag)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_CLASS
				WHERE "Account Classification.Primary (Flag)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qAccount Classification.Primary (Flag)__3"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Account Classification.Classification Category"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_CLASS
				WHERE "Account Classification.Classification Category" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qAccount Classification.Classification Category__4"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Account Classification.Assignment Criteria"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_CLASS
				WHERE "Account Classification.Assignment Criteria" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qAccount Classification.Assignment Criteria__5"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "Account Classification.Status"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_CLASS
				WHERE "Account Classification.Status" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qAccount Classification.Status__2"
	FROM OSC_DATA_EXTRACTS.SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_CLASS
	) AS t
UNPIVOT(NullCount FOR pCol IN (
			"pACCOUNT_ID__1"
			,"pAccount Classification.Primary (Flag)__3"
			,"pAccount Classification.Classification Category__4"
			,"pAccount Classification.Assignment Criteria__5"
			,"pAccount Classification.Status__2"
			)) AS p
UNPIVOT(ExampleData FOR qCol IN (
			"qACCOUNT_ID__1"
			,"qAccount Classification.Primary (Flag)__3"
			,"qAccount Classification.Classification Category__4"
			,"qAccount Classification.Assignment Criteria__5"
			,"qAccount Classification.Status__2"
			)) AS q
WHERE CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) = CAST(SUBSTRING(qCol, CHARINDEX('__', qCol) + 2) AS INTEGER)

UNION ALL

SELECT TableName
	,TotalRows
	,SUBSTRING(pCol, 2, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) - 1) AS ColName
	,CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) AS ColPos
	,NullCount
	,CAST(CAST(NullCount AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) / NULLIF(CAST(TotalRows AS DECIMAL(12, 2)), 0) * 100.00 AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) AS NullPct
	,ExampleData
FROM (
	SELECT 'SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_TREENODE' AS TableName
		,COUNT(*) AS TotalRows
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("ACCOUNT_ID (Parent)") AS "pACCOUNT_ID (Parent)__1"
		,COUNT(*) - COUNT("ACCOUNT_ID (Child)") AS "pACCOUNT_ID (Child)__2"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "ACCOUNT_ID (Parent)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_TREENODE
				WHERE "ACCOUNT_ID (Parent)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qACCOUNT_ID (Parent)__1"
		,IFNULL((
				SELECT TOP 1 "ACCOUNT_ID (Child)"
				FROM SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_TREENODE
				WHERE "ACCOUNT_ID (Child)" IS NOT NULL
				), '') AS "qACCOUNT_ID (Child)__2"
	FROM OSC_DATA_EXTRACTS.SV_OSC_P_T_ACCNT_TREENODE
	) AS t
UNPIVOT(NullCount FOR pCol IN (
			"pACCOUNT_ID (Parent)__1"
			,"pACCOUNT_ID (Child)__2"
			)) AS p
UNPIVOT(ExampleData FOR qCol IN (
			"qACCOUNT_ID (Parent)__1"
			,"qACCOUNT_ID (Child)__2"
			)) AS q
WHERE CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) = CAST(SUBSTRING(qCol, CHARINDEX('__', qCol) + 2) AS INTEGER)

SELECT TableName
	,TotalRows
	,SUBSTRING(pCol, 2, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) - 1) AS ColName
	,CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) AS ColPos
	,NullCount
	,CAST(CAST(NullCount AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) / NULLIF(CAST(TotalRows AS DECIMAL(12, 2)), 0) * 100.00 AS DECIMAL(12, 2)) AS NullPct
	,ExampleData

			,"qProduct.BL__9"
			,"qProduct.Created Timestamp__7"
			,"qPRODUCT_ID__2"
			)) AS q
WHERE CAST(SUBSTRING(pCol, CHARINDEX('__', pCol) + 2) AS INTEGER) = CAST(SUBSTRING(qCol, CHARINDEX('__', qCol) + 2) AS INTEGER)
ORDER BY TableName
	,ColPos;
